[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m604[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m606[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The heap-buffer-overflow arises because the code that recognizes JSON literals [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m“true”, “false”, “null”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m checks the remaining buffer size with too-small [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstants. For each literal, it does:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - increment the input pointer one character at a time [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `*[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor each expected character[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - but only verifies that `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < N` where N is one less than the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnumber of required subsequent bytes  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   As a result, when exactly N bytes remain, the guard evaluates false and the code[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreads past the end on the final `++state.ptr` access.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue to use the same `*[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mit’s pervasive [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrough `json_parse_ex`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On success, `[0m[1;35mnew_value[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&state, …, json_boolean[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` must remain unchanged for [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid literals.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We’re only tightening the buffer-length pre-checks; no other control flow or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merror paths are altered.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed Patch Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `src/shadowsocks/src/json.c`, within `json_parse_ex`:  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Locate the `case [0m[32m't'[0m[39m:` block [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m600[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Change its guard from  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'r'[0m[39m ||[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        to[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'r'[0m[39m ||[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Locate the `case [0m[32m'n'[0m[39m:` block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe [0m[32m"null"[0m[39m literal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Change its guard from `<[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m` to `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmatching the three-character “ull” sequence[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Locate the `case [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m:` block [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m616[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Change its guard from  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'a'[0m[39m ||[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'l'[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m's'[0m[39m ||[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        to[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'a'[0m[39m ||[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'l'[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m's'[0m[39m ||[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. No other functions or harness code are modified.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Re-run existing unit tests and fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`json_fuzz`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to confirm the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow is eliminated and no regressions occur.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By increasing each numeric bound by exactly [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, we ensure there are sufficient [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes for all `++state.ptr` advances.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We preserve the literal-matching approach and all error paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `goto [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39me_unknown_value`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We avoid any changes to the fuzzer harness or utility functions—only the JSON [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser itself is hardened.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Slightly more input will now be rejected as `e_unknown_value` where previously[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit caused an overflow. That is intended: incomplete literals are invalid JSON.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No performance impact: a single extra integer comparison per literal.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No impact on supported functionality beyond stricter validation.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzz `json_parse_ex` with previously crashing inputs—no leaks or overflows [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould remain.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run the full test suite to ensure JSON parsing of valid inputs is unchanged.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBy following these steps, we close the off-by-one window for each literal without [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maltering overall parser semantics.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - AddressSanitizer reported a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read beyond the end of an allocated [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m-byte [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion during execution of `json_parse_ex` at json.[0m[1;92mc:620:29[0m[39m.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack trace shows the overflow occurs while handling JSON values [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mspecifically the branch for the character ‘n’[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, then bubbles up through [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_parse`, into the LLVMFuzzer callback, and finally aborts.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Observations from Initial Log  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The faulty access is at address `[0m[1;36m0x5020000000b5[0m[39m`, immediately after a [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m-byte [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x5020000000b0[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x5020000000b5[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The error is triggered in the code path for the ‘n’ case [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpresumably parsing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`null` or a variant[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The sanitizer output shows “SCARINESS: [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m” and pinpoints `json_parse_ex` line [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m620[0m[39m.[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `src/json.c`, at around line [0m[1;36m630[0m[39m, the guard for parsing the literal ‘null’ [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwas modified.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Original code:  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m ||[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Patched code:  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m ||[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change intended to ensure at least [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes remain before advancing and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatching “u”, “l”, “l”.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Result After Patch  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer was rerun under AddressSanitizer with the same command line.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - An identical heap‐buffer‐overflow was reported at the same location in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_parse_ex` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjson.[0m[1;92mc:620:29[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The shadow bytes and stack trace are virtually unchanged, confirming the same [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds read survives the patch.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The parsing logic around the ‘n’ case in `json_parse_ex`, including how [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`state.ptr` and `end` are computed and updated.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adjacent branches for other literals [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`true`, `false`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to compare guard logic [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand buffer checks.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer is determined.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Each of the three branches for JSON literals [0m[1;39m([0m[39m“true”, “false”, “null”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madvances the input pointer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`state.ptr`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m multiple times to validate each character [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the literal.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing guard for available bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`end - state.ptr < N`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m underestimates [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe number of bytes needed, so when `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == N`, the guard passes but [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma subsequent `*[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` reads one past `end`, triggering a [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap‐buffer‐overflow.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Specifically:  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • “true” has [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m characters but uses `< [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` as the guard [0m[1;39m([0m[39mneeds `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • “false” has [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m characters but uses `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` as the guard [0m[1;39m([0m[39mneeds `< [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • “null” has [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m characters; it was originally `< [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mneeds `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and was [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatched, but the fixes for “true” and “false” were not applied.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After matching the literal, `state.ptr` must point to the last character of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe literal, so that the outer parsing loop’s `++state.ptr` will move to the next [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon‐literal character.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The call to `[0m[1;35mnew_value[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` must remain after all pointer increments to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocate the correct JSON node.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Error handling via `goto e_unknown_value` on malformed or truncated literals [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmust be unchanged.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Comprehensive Patch Steps  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `src/json.c` and locate the three literal‐parsing `case` blocks in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_parse_ex`:  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - case [0m[32m't'[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m600[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m607[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - case [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m616[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m620[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - case [0m[32m'n'[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m631[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m635[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Modify the byte‐remaining guards as follows:  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - For “true”: change `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` to `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - For “false”: change `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` to `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - For “null”: ensure it reads `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthis was already [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplied in the last patch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Leave the subsequent `*[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` checks, `[0m[1;35mnew_value[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls, and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`flags |= flag_next` logic untouched.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Rebuild the library and rerun the fuzzer under AddressSanitizer to confirm no[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfurther heap‐buffer‐overflow is reported in these branches.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification & Preservation of Existing Behavior  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tightening the guards to match the actual number of pointer increments ensures[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat truncated inputs will hit `goto e_unknown_value` rather than reading past the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid inputs [0m[1;39m([0m[39m“true”[0m[35m/[0m[39m“false”[0m[35m/[0m[39m“null”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m have sufficient length so the new guards [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdo not alter successful parsing.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing error‐paths, memory‐allocation calls, and post‐literal [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstate‐updates remain in place, preserving the rest of the JSON parser’s control [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mflow.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This minimal change addresses the reported vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSCARINESS [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without modifying harness or test code, avoiding unintended side‐effects.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side‐Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No functionality is removed; only truncated‐literal handling becomes slightly [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmore strict [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbut still properly reports syntax errors[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Performance impact is negligible, limited to one integer comparison per [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mliteral parse.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No existing tests should fail, since valid literals are unaffected.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other literal parsing branches [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., numbers, strings[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are untouched; [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmonitoring can ensure no regressions elsewhere.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References in Codebase  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The “true” and “false” branches immediately precede the “null” branch and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollow the same pattern. Adjusting them symmetrically ensures consistency across [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall literal handlers.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar off‐by‐one fixes in JSON parsers often require matching guard [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthresholds to `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mliteral[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` rather than `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mliteral[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`; here we align [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meach guard to the full literal length.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo changes to external libraries, harness files, or test code are required. After [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplying this patch, the reported heap‐buffer‐overflow in `json_parse_ex` will be [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolved.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
